### [234] [ElephantAgent: Contextual State Continuity in Agentic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01919)
*Jiankai Jin,Xiangzheng Zhang,Zhao Liu,Wenzhuo Xu,Dongdong Yang,Deyue Zhang,Quanchen Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ElephantAgent是一个通过强制上下文状态连续性来防御上下文状态中毒的协议，它利用可信硬件复制和线性化账本检测状态篡改，并提供历史可追溯性以实现事后审计和状态恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体系统依赖外部工具和持久化记忆，但引入了新的攻击面（工具描述符中毒、记忆中毒），现有系统缺乏对智能体上下文状态的可验证连续性，导致状态篡改难以被发现。

Method: 定义上下文状态为安全关键子集；每次查询前重新计算本地上下文状态摘要并与授权摘要比对；利用复制的可信硬件维护线性化授权状态转换账本；提供历史可追溯性支持事后审计和状态回滚。

Result: 能够检测带外状态篡改（通过摘要验证）和带内语义滥用（通过历史可追溯性和恢复机制），为智能体系统提供上下文状态完整性保障。

Conclusion: ElephantAgent将状态连续性保护扩展到智能体系统的演化上下文状态，有效防御了上下文状态中毒攻击，为构建安全可靠的智能体系统提供了关键基础设施。

Abstract: Agentic systems enhance their capabilities by invoking external tools and maintaining persistent memory. However, these external dependencies introduce novel attack surfaces. Recent tool and memory poisoning attacks show that maliciously crafted tool descriptors and poisoned memory can covertly bias agent behavior. These threats reflect a deeper issue: the lack of verifiable continuity in the agent's contextual state for planning and execution. We present ElephantAgent, a protocol that enforces Contextual State Continuity to defend against contextual state poisoning. Inspired by prior state-continuity mechanisms (e.g., Nimble), ElephantAgent extends this protection to the evolving contextual state of agentic systems. We define the contextual state as the bounded, security-critical subset of the agent's entire context (e.g., tool state and memory). Before processing each query, ElephantAgent recomputes the digest of the local contextual state and verifies it against the latest authorized digest. Using replicated trusted hardware, ElephantAgent maintains a linearizable ledger of authorized contextual state transitions and detects out-of-band state tampering. To handle in-band semantic abuse, ElephantAgent additionally provides Historical Traceability, enabling conditional post-hoc audit and recovery to a known-good prior state.

### [235] [A-TMA: Decoupling State-Aware Memory Failures in Long-Term Agent Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01935)
*Zitong Shi,Yixuan Tang,Anthony Kum Hoe Tung*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ATMA，一种状态感知的覆盖层，用于解决LLM记忆系统中新旧事实混淆的"幽灵记忆"问题。通过在记忆库维护、检索和答案生成三个层面显式处理状态信息，ATMA显著提升了冲突事实处理能力，并将时间F1从0.0295提升至0.1705。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM记忆系统无法区分当前事实、历史事实和变迁事实，导致"幽灵记忆"问题——新旧信息混淆共存，检索时混合输出，误导问答模型。作者认为应从记忆库维护、检索和答案生成三个层面理解和优化记忆系统。

Method: 提出ATMA，一种状态感知覆盖层：(1) 在记忆库中保留被取代的记录和变迁记录；(2) 为查询请求的状态视图构建证据包；(3) 向QA暴露当前、历史和变迁标签。同时构建LTP基准数据集用于独立评估记忆库、检索和答案层面的失败。

Result: 在LTP数据集上，Graphiti+ATMA将冲突准确率绝对提升0.240；在LoCoMo上，时间F1从0.0295提升至0.1705。但增益依赖于宿主系统。

Conclusion: 显式的状态角色设计可以减少被最终QA准确率掩盖的记忆失败，呼吁对记忆库、检索和答案层面的失败进行解耦评估。

Abstract: Long term memory lets LLM agents act as persistent assistants, but user facts change. A useful memory system must know what is true now, what used to be true, and what changed. We study \emph{ghost memory}, a state coordination failure in which old, current, and transition facts coexist in the memory bank, remain mixed during retrieval, and mislead the answer model. We argue that memory systems should be understood and optimized from three levels: bank maintenance, retrieval, and answer time resolution. We propose ATMA, a state aware overlay for existing memory systems. ATMA keeps superseded and transition records in the bank, builds evidence packets for the query's requested state view, and exposes current, historical, and transition labels to QA. We further call for decoupled evaluation of bank, retrieval, and answer level failures, since final QA accuracy can hide where ghost memory occurs. To make this failure measurable, we build LTP (LoCoMo Temporal Plus), a conflict heavy benchmark for ghost memory, and evaluate on LoCoMo for long conversation generalization. On LTP, Graphiti+ATMA improves conflict accuracy by 0.240 absolute over Graphiti. On LoCoMo, Graphiti+ATMA raises temporal F1 from 0.0295 to 0.1705. The gains are host dependent, but they indicate that explicit state roles can reduce memory failures hidden by final QA accuracy.

### [236] [Atomic Task Graph: A Unified Framework for Agentic Planning and Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01942)
*Yue Zhang,Sihan Chen,Ziwen Huang,Hanyun Cui,Kangye Ji,Zhi Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出原子任务图（ATG）框架，通过显式图结构进行任务规划与执行，支持依赖暴露、并行执行、错误定位与修复，仅用7B-8B小模型即在三个交互基准上超越强基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体方法依赖大模型或任务微调，成本高且泛化差；基于提示的控制虽无需训练，但子任务间依赖关系隐含在文本轨迹中，已验证的中间结果难以复用。

Method: ATG维护显式图结构暴露依赖关系：规划阶段递归分解高层任务为子任务，形成可追踪演化的有向无环图序列；执行阶段利用依赖关系实现独立分支并行执行，检测到失败时基于图演化历史定位错误源并仅修复受影响区域。

Result: 仅使用7B-8B小模型，在三个交互式基准测试中，ATG在成功率和执行效率上一致优于强基线方法。

Conclusion: 显式图结构控制框架可以有效提升小模型在多步复杂任务中的表现，兼顾训练自由、计算高效和跨任务泛化能力。

Abstract: LLM-based agents have shown strong potential for solving complex multi-step tasks, yet existing performance improvements often rely on either scaling to larger backbone models or task-specific fine-tuning. The former incurs substantial computational costs, while the latter typically generalizes poorly across different tasks. Although prompt-based control is training-free and broadly applicable, existing methods still leave input-output dependencies between subtasks implicit in textual trajectories, making verified intermediate results difficult to reuse. To address these limitations, we propose Atomic Task Graph (ATG), a unified control framework for planning and execution. Specifically, ATG maintains an explicit graph to expose dependencies and support reuse. During planning, it recursively decomposes a high-level task into subtasks, forming a sequence of directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) whose evolution can be traced. During execution, the dependencies exposed by ATG allow independent branches to be executed in parallel, thereby improving execution efficiency. When failures are detected, ATG leverages the graph evolution history to localize the error source and repair only the affected region, preserving validated regions unchanged. Experiments show that ATG consistently outperforms strong baselines in success rate and execution efficiency across three interactive benchmarks using only 7B-8B backbones.

Abstract: Ontology learning (OL) aims to automatically construct structured knowledge models from text, yet progress remains fragmented across methods, domains, and evaluation practices. Despite decades of research, OL lacks a shared infrastructure for systematic evaluation and ontology access. This absence has hindered progress and fragmented research, leaving the central challenges of OL largely unaddressed. We introduce OntoLearner, a modular, cross-domain, and first-of-its-kind framework that unifies ontology access, large language model (LLM)-driven learning pipelines, and standardized benchmarking. OntoLearner releases 180 machine-readable ontologies spanning 22 domains and provides pipeline-ready datasets with train/dev/test splits for three core OL tasks: term typing, taxonomy discovery, and non-taxonomic relation extraction. Using this infrastructure, we conduct a large-scale empirical study of OL, evaluating 22 retrieval models and 12 LLMs across domains and tasks. The results converge on a finding that reframes the central challenge of OL: failure modes scale with ontological complexity rather than model size or architectural sophistication. The primary bottleneck is not model capability, but a structural mismatch between how models encode knowledge and how ontologies organize it. These findings establish that effective OL is reachable through the cross-domain, multi-task benchmarking enabled by OntoLearner. OntoLearner is open-source (MIT license) at https://github.com/sciknoworg/OntoLearner/.

### [238] [Multimodal Knowledge Edit-Scoped Generalization for Online Recursive MLLM Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01978)
*Siyuan Li,Youyuan Zhang,Ruitong Liu,Junxi Wang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出ScopeEdit，一种范围感知的在线多模态知识编辑方法，通过将每次更新分解为模态局部吸收分支和证据门控共享泛化分支，在正交低秩空间中实现范围分离的写入，有效平衡了跨模态泛化与无关内容保护，同时保持编辑可靠性、稳定性和在线效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线多模态知识编辑器主要关注编辑可靠性和长期稳定性，但很少控制每次编辑的语义边界。研究发现编辑存在"范围差距"：实例级成功既不能保证有效跨模态变体迁移，也无法防止泄露到无关输入。因此需要重新定义问题，从单纯纠正实例转向控制每次编辑的传播边界。

Method: ScopeEdit将每次更新分解为两个分支：(1) 模态局部吸收分支 - 支持稳定的编辑吸收；(2) 证据门控共享泛化分支 - 仅在视觉和文本证据充分对齐时才允许跨模态传播。两个分支在正交低秩空间中执行范围分离的写入几何，并通过Sherman-Morrison递归维护分支级预处理器，实现恒定每次编辑开销。

Result: 在多种基准、长时编辑流、不同MLLM骨干网络、真实场景VLKEB以及复杂视觉-语言架构上的实验表明，ScopeEdit在范围内跨模态迁移与范围外局部性之间取得了更好的权衡，同时保持了编辑可靠性、稳定性和在线效率。

Conclusion: ScopeEdit通过显式建模编辑的语义边界，有效解决了多模态知识编辑中的范围泛化问题，为在线MLLM编辑提供了更可控、更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Online multimodal knowledge editing requires injecting a continual stream of visual-textual corrections into multimodal large language models (MLLMs) with bounded overhead and minimal disruption to unrelated behaviors. Existing editors mainly emphasize edit reliability and long-horizon stability, but rarely control the semantic boundary of each edit. Our pilot analyses of post-edit behaviors and internal neuronal activities reveal a scope gap behind reliable edits: instance-level success neither guarantees transfer to valid cross-modal variants nor prevents leakage to unrelated inputs, while edit-related cross-modal responses concentrate in deeper semantic layers. Therefore, we formulate Edit-Scoped Generalization, reframing online MLLM editing from merely correcting an instance to controlling the propagation boundary of each edit. To this end, we propose ScopeEdit, a scope-aware online editor that decomposes each update into a modality-local absorption branch and an evidence-gated shared generalization branch. The local branch supports stable edit absorption, whereas the shared branch enables cross-modal propagation only when visual and textual evidence are sufficiently aligned. Both branches perform scope-separated write geometries in orthogonal low-rank spaces and maintain branch-wise preconditioners via Sherman--Morrison recursions, yielding constant per-edit overhead. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks, long-horizon edit streams, MLLM backbones, real-world VLKEB scenarios, and complex vision-language architectures show that ScopeEdit consistently improves the trade-off between in-scope cross-modal transfer and out-of-scope locality, while preserving edit reliability, stability and online efficiency. Our code is available at https://github.com/lab-klc/ScopeEdit.

### [239] [Episodic-to-Semantic Consolidation Without Identity Drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01988)
*Xue Qin,Simin Luan,Cong Yang,Zhijun Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向长期运行自适应智能体的知识整合方法，将记忆整合视为从情节记忆到语义记忆的确定性函数，而非改变智能体身份的操作，从而在保留加密认证身份不变的前提下实现知识更新，实验证明可减少约79.82%的无效规划尝试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期运行的自适应智能体面临知识整合（知识合并）与信息完整性之间的结构性张力。传统方法将整合视为改变智能体本身的操作（如微调模型、重写提示等），这在受监管的自动化部署中成为隐患，因为智能体需在加密认证身份不变的承诺和审计合约下运作。

Method: 将记忆整合定义为从情节记忆（M^ep）到语义记忆（M^sem）的确定性函数 f，输出为独立可寻址的语义知识层；智能体身份哈希不读取 M^sem，因此知识更新不改变认证身份。给出了智能体表征的形式化描述、通过身份清单哈希输入集的结构引理证明身份不变性，以及确定性聚合算法，其输出为可审计的数据库行，带有显式置信度和支持事件溯源。

Result: 合成实验验证了字段级正确性、整合前后身份字节级相等，以及平均减少79.82%的无效规划尝试（95% BCa置信区间[78.02%, 81.49%]，10个随机种子），对比校准的贝叶斯收缩基线。

Conclusion: 该构造为自治智能体提供了一种知识更新规范：智能体以可查询事实的形式积累经验，同时其认证身份在运行生命周期内保持字节级不变。

Abstract: Long-running adaptive intelligent agents face a structural tension between knowledge consolidation and information integrity. Memory consolidation is conventionally treated as an agent-changing operation: a model is fine-tuned, a prompt rewritten, a policy distilled, or a reflection appended to the context that governs future behaviour. In regulated autonomic deployment this is a liability because the agent operates under commitments and audit contracts that bind to a specific, cryptographically certified identity. We propose to treat consolidation not as a mutation of the planner or the identity manifest, but as a deterministic function f: M^ep -> M^sem over episodic memory whose output is a separately addressable semantic knowledge layer; the identity hash does not read M^sem, so consolidation updates knowledge without changing the agent's certified identity. We give a formal account of the agent representation, prove identity invariance through a structural lemma on the manifest's hash-input set, specify a deterministic aggregation algorithm whose outputs are auditable database rows with explicit confidence and supporting-event provenance, and validate the construction with synthetic experiments demonstrating per-field correctness, byte-equal identity across consolidation passes, and a mean 79.82% reduction in unproductive planner attempts (95% BCa CI [78.02%, 81.49%] across 10 seeds) against a calibrated Bayesian-shrunk baseline. The construction is a knowledge-update discipline for autonomic agents in which lessons accumulate as queryable facts while the agent's certified identity remains byte-equal across its operational lifetime, with an embodied service agent as the running case study.

### [241] [InduceKV: Fixed-Footprint Continual Adaptation of Multimodal LLMs via Inducing KV Memories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02010)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型需要在有限部署资源下持续适应新任务/领域，但传统方法（重复参数更新、不断扩大的回放存储）会积累大量适应状态，导致内存开销不断增长，难以满足固定部署足迹的约束。

Method: 提出 InduceKV：（1）将选中的训练前缀存储为注意力就绪的记忆条目，包含冻结检索键和紧凑的逐层 KV 载荷；（2）采用双层选择机制构建紧凑诱导集：先进行轻量校准使检索更适配，再平衡当前任务似然、基于锚点的保留性和检索空间中的覆盖率来筛选记忆。

Result: 在任务增量指令微调、持续 VQA、领域增量适应和终身多模态指令微调等多个设置下，InduceKV 在匹配内存预算的情况下持续优于 PEFT、MoE、回放和提示检索基线。还提供了骨干网络匹配、CoIN 阶段-1、计算量匹配及可扩展性诊断等分析。

Conclusion: InduceKV 在固定内存预算下实现了有效的持续适应，且其增益并非来自更强的骨干网络、单纯的回放或无限的候选池，证明了基于检索的外部记忆方法是可行的方向。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet continual improvement under bounded deployment footprint remains difficult because repeated parameter updates or growing replay stores can accumulate adaptation state over time. We study fixed-footprint continual adaptation: the deployed adaptation state is kept under a fixed memory budget, while the backbone model is left unchanged and task-specific updates are externalized. We propose InduceKV, a retrieval-based method that stores each selected training prefix as an attention-ready memory entry, consisting of a frozen retrieval key and compact layerwise key--value (KV) payloads that can be appended to the model's self-attention cache. Under a strict memory budget, InduceKV constructs a compact inducing set through bilevel selection: a lightweight calibration is fit for retrieval, while the selected memory balances current-task likelihood, anchor-based retention, and coverage in the frozen retrieval space. Across task-incremental instruction tuning, continual VQA, domain-incremental adaptation, and lifelong multimodal instruction tuning, InduceKV consistently improves over PEFT, MoE, replay, and prompt-retrieval baselines under matched memory budgets. We further report backbone-matched, stage-1 CoIN, compute-matched, and scalability diagnostics, showing that the gains are not due to a stronger backbone, replay alone, or an unbounded candidate pool.

*Qianyu Chen,Canran Xiao,Runxuan Tang*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需回放的依赖约束持续学习框架RCL，解决了多模态大模型在持续学习中"隐藏的证据使用遗忘"问题——即模型答案正确但证据来源发生偏移。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续学习指标仅关注答案正确性，忽视了多模态模型在持续适应过程中证据使用稳定性这一关键问题。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models must continually adapt to evolving tasks and domains, yet standard continual learning metrics mainly measure whether old answers remain correct, leaving the stability of multimodal grounding largely unexamined. We study this overlooked failure mode and ask whether a continually adapted MLLM can preserve not only what it answers, but also how it uses visual, textual, OCR, chart, and document evidence. We identify \emph{hidden evidence-use forgetting}, where answer accuracy is retained while the model silently shifts toward different or less grounded evidence channels, and propose \textsc{RCL}, a replay-free reliance-constrained continual learning framework. \textsc{RCL} freezes the previous checkpoint as a behavioral reference, estimates teacher and student evidence-reliance profiles through counterfactual channel interventions, and jointly optimizes task learning, prediction preservation, and reliance preservation without adding inference-time cost. Across CoIN, COAST, MCITlib, and an evidence-sensitive multimodal stream, \textsc{RCL} consistently improves final performance and reduces forgetting over replay-free, PEFT, routing, and memory-assisted baselines, while substantially lowering modality reliance drift, dominant evidence flips, and hidden forgetting rates. These results suggest that robust continual multimodal learning requires preserving the evidence path behind correct answers, not merely the answers themselves.

### [243] [PACE: A Proxy for Agentic Capability Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02032)
*Yueqi Song,Lintang Sutawika,Jiarui Liu,Lindia Tjuatja,Jiayi Geng,Yunze Xiao,Daniel Lee,Aditya Bharat Soni,Vincent Lo,Xiang Yue,Graham Neubig*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PACE框架，通过从非智能体评测中筛选少量原子能力实例来预测昂贵智能体基准测试的性能，在不到1%的成本下实现MAE<4%、Spearman>0.80的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体基准测试（如SWE-Bench、GAIA）评估成本高昂、耗时且基础设施复杂（单次数千美元、数天），而传统非智能体评测快速廉价。作者希望利用廉价评测预测昂贵智能体性能，以降低评估开销。

Method: PACE框架：从原子能力评测池中，结合"目标相关局部选择"和"全局信息全局选择"两种互补策略筛选紧凑子集，通过回归模型将模型在子集上的得分映射到目标智能体基准得分。

Result: 在14个模型、4个智能体基准、19个非智能体基准上，PACE-Bench的LOOCV MAE<4%，Spearman相关性>0.80，模型配对排序准确率约85%，成本仅为完整评估的不到1%。

Abstract: Evaluating LLM agents on benchmarks like SWE-Bench and GAIA can be expensive, time-consuming, and requires complex infrastructure. A single evaluation can cost thousands of dollars and take days to complete. In contrast, non-agentic LLM benchmarks that test individual capabilities (e.g., reasoning, code generation) are fast and cheap to run. In this paper, we investigate whether performance on expensive agentic benchmarks can be accurately predicted by the performance on a small, carefully selected subset of atomic evaluation instances. We introduce PACE, a framework that constructs proxy benchmarks by selecting instances from existing non-agentic evaluations whose aggregate scores most reliably predict model performances on agentic benchmarks. Given a pool of candidate instances spanning atomic capabilities, PACE fits a regression that maps a model's scores on a compact subset of source instances to its score on the target agentic benchmark. The subset itself is curated by combining two complementary instance-selection strategies, target-relevance local selection and globally informative global selection. We apply PACE to the 4 target agentic benchmarks in this paper, which yields PACE-Bench, the concrete proxy benchmark that we evaluate in the paper. Experiments across 14 models, 4 agentic benchmarks, and 19 non-agentic benchmarks show that PACE-Bench predicts agentic scores with leave-one-out cross-validation (LOOCV) mean absolute error (MAE) under 4%, Spearman correlation above 0.80, and pairwise model-ranking accuracy around 85%, all at much less than 1% of the full agentic evaluation cost. We further analyze the selected proxy instances, revealing which skills each agentic benchmark uniquely demands. PACE enables practitioners to obtain reliable estimates of agentic performance during model development, selection, and routing, without the overhead of full agent evaluation.

### [244] [Algebraic Model Counting for Global Analysis of Optimal Decision Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02069)
*Hiroki Arimura*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出代数决策树计数（ADTC）框架，通过半环上的和-积计算统一优化、计数和采样等分析任务，实现对最优和近优决策树的穷举分析，时间复杂度为O*(n^{O(Δ)})，并引入模型行为张量处理多指标约束，最终通过emtrees软件在真实数据集上展示其促进基于证据的模型选择能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保可解释AI中的模型可靠性需要对假设空间进行全局评估，现有方法缺乏对最优和近优决策树进行穷举分析的形式化框架。

Method: 受知识表示中的代数模型计数（AMC）启发，将优化、计数和采样统一为半环R上的和-积计算；提出动态规划算法实现O*(n^{O(Δ)})时间复杂度；引入模型行为张量，通过张量半环上的卷积积聚合多指标半环值，构建全局模型画像。

Result: 提出ADTC框架，算法时间复杂度为O*(n^{O(Δ)})（n为特征数，Δ为最大深度）；开发了emtrees软件，在真实数据集上验证了框架的有效性。

Conclusion: ADTC通过代数方法高效构建模型全局景观与权衡关系（如精度、大小、公平性），为敏感领域的基于证据的模型选择提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Ensuring model reliability in Explainable AI requires a global assessment of the hypothesis space. We propose a formal framework for the exhaustive analysis of optimal and near-optimal decision trees, called Algebraic Decision Tree Counting (ADTC). Inspired by Algebraic Model Counting (AMC) in knowledge representation, ADTC reformulates diverse analytical tasks, such as optimization, counting, and sampling, into a unified sum-of-products computation over a semiring $R$. While the hypothesis space of decision trees is doubly exponential with respect to the maximum depth $Δ$, our dynamic programming algorithm achieves $O^*(n^{O(Δ)})$ time complexity in the number of features $n$, where $O^*$ suppresses polynomial factors. To handle complex constraints consisting of multiple tree metrics, we introduce model behavior tensors that aggregate semiring values via convolution products over a tensor semiring. This algebraic approach efficiently constructs a model profile that captures the global landscape and trade-offs between criteria such as accuracy, size, and fairness. We demonstrate the utility of our software, emtrees, on real-world datasets, illustrating how ADTC facilitates evidence-based model selection in sensitive domains.

*Ya Gao,Pekka Marttinen*

TL;DR: Maven是一个强化学习框架，通过可编辑的证据记忆和动作级状态转换奖励机制，在长上下文推理中优于传统结果奖励RL和证据识别基线方法。

Method: 提出Maven框架，定义答案条件化的证据状态价值，对add（边际增益+事后贡献）、link（证据协同）、drop（误导移除后改善）三种动作分别设计状态转换奖励，并在GRPO中分配给对应动作跨度。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning requires models to locate, revise, and synthesize evidence distributed across lengthy inputs. Existing long-context RL methods usually reward final answers or static evidence extraction, offering little feedback on how intermediate actions change the model's evidence state. We propose Maven, a reinforcement learning framework with an editable evidence memory. Maven defines an answer-conditioned evidence-state value and rewards action-level state transitions: add actions are credited by marginal gain and hindsight contribution, link actions by evidence synergy, and drop actions by improved answer support after removing misleading evidence. These rewards are assigned to the corresponding action spans in GRPO. Across Llama and Qwen models on LongBench v2, LongReason, and RULER, Maven outperforms outcome-only RL and evidence-identification baselines, producing more sufficient evidence sets and lower distractor retention.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HSSM依赖固定长度或相似性检测的分块方式，无法对齐数据内在时序结构；作者主张分块应由预测误差驱动，因为它更直接指示何时需要长程上下文。

Method: 提出SUNTA：1) 解耦训练策略保留惊奇信号，避免端到端训练中的层次坍塌；2) 使用内部不一致性作为自上而下的惊奇度量，在想象推演中确定分块边界。

Abstract: Hierarchical state-space models (HSSMs) offer a promising approach to long-horizon prediction by segmenting sequences into temporal chunks. However, their performance hinges on how chunk boundaries are determined. While prior HSSMs typically rely on fixed-length chunking or similarity-based boundary detection, these methods often misalign with the intrinsic temporal structure of the data. We argue that chunking should instead be driven by prediction errors, which more directly indicate when longer-range context becomes necessary. Nevertheless, integrating surprise-based chunking into HSSMs introduces critical challenges, including hierarchical collapse during end-to-end training and the absence of surprise signals during open-loop prediction. To address these issues, we propose Surprise-based Nested Temporal Abstraction (SUNTA), a method that employs a decoupled training strategy to preserve surprise signals and uses internal inconsistency as a top-down surprise metric to determine chunk boundaries within imagined rollouts. Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ContextNext 是一种为AI代理提供上下文治理的开放规范，在检索之前确保知识工件的可追溯性、版本完整性和审计能力，实验表明其在抗过时版本攻击和检索确定性上优于传统方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ContextNext规范：结合类型化Markdown文档、确定性集合代数选择器、contextnest:// URI引用、SHA-256哈希链版本历史、图级检查点、通过MCP协议实时数据源以及代理上下文消费的审计追踪。

Abstract: Autonomous AI agents increasingly depend on external knowledge stores, yet most retrieval pipelines provide relevance without durable guarantees of provenance, version identity, integrity, traceability, or point-in-time reconstruction. We formalize this as context governance and present ContextNext, an open specification and reference implementation for governed AI-consumable knowledge vaults. ContextNext does not replace Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG); it supplies the governance layer beneath retrieval, determining which artifacts are approved, current, attributable, and integrity-verified before retrieval systems operate over them.
  The specification combines typed Markdown documents with metadata, deterministic set-algebraic selectors, contextnest:// URI references, SHA-256 hash-chained version histories, graph-level checkpoints, source nodes for live data through the Model Context Protocol (MCP), and audit traces of agent context consumption. These mechanisms let organizations reconstruct which knowledge versions informed an agent output and whether those versions were AI-eligible when consumed.
  We report first empirical results from two controlled experiments. In a stale-version attack isolating the governance-versus-retrieval failure mode, governed selection strictly Pareto-dominates BM25 sparse retrieval, with higher answer-quality pass rate (97% versus 93-90%) at about one-third the input-token cost. In a retrieval-determinism experiment over a 1,060-document corpus, deterministic selectors and BM25 return stable document sets across repeated identical queries (Jaccard 1.0), while a dense+HNSW baseline is non-deterministic on 80% of queries (mean Jaccard 0.611, worst case 0.210). These results suggest that context governance addresses failure modes retrieval quality alone is not designed to resolve. We release a core engine, CLI, and MCP server under open licenses.

### [249] [Coding-agents can replicate scientific machine learning papers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02134)
*Atharva Hans,Ilias Bilionis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Paper-replication工作流，使编码智能体能够以可验证的方式复现科学机器学习论文中的计算性声明，通过将声明转化为可追踪目标、重建方法、运行实验并链接证据，最终通过验证检查完成复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学机器学习论文通常包含计算性声明（如误差小于5%），但仅靠提示词引导编码智能体复现这些声明，无法可靠地保存进展或验证生成证据是否真正支持论文声明，需要更系统化的流程来确保复现的可追溯性和可验证性。

Method: Paper-replication工作流将每个论文声明设为可记录证据的目标，智能体需记录这些目标、重建论文方法、运行计算实验、将输出链接到来源并与论文声明进行比对、在复现报告中记录匹配证据的位置，最后通过验证检查才能完成。

Result: 在四篇科学机器学习论文的12次独立运行中，所有工作空间均通过完成检查，158个记录目标均被报告覆盖。但不同运行在目标划分方式、数值忠实度、复现耗时、中间执行替换次数及证据接受规则上存在差异。

Conclusion: Paper-replication使复现的完成依赖于工作空间中的证据和验证检查，而非智能体的最终消息，提高了复现过程的可靠性和可审计性，但不同运行的差异性也揭示了自动化复现中存在的灵活性挑战。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning papers typically make computational claims, e.g., that the relative mean square error is less than 5% or that the 95% predictive credible interval covers the test data. A coding agent can be prompted to replicate those claims from paper materials alone, but the prompt does not by itself reliably preserve progress or check whether generated evidence supports the paper's claims. We introduce Paper-replication, a workflow that makes each selected paper claim a target with recorded evidence, and implement it as a coding-agent skill. The workflow makes the agent record those targets, reconstruct the paper's method, run computational experiments, link generated outputs to provenance and comparisons with the paper's claims, record where matched evidence appears in the replication report, and pass validation checks before completion. We evaluate Paper-replication on twelve independent runs across four scientific machine learning papers. All twelve workspaces pass the completion gate, and all 158 recorded targets are matched with report coverage. Even in this completed workspace state, repeated runs differ in how papers are divided into targets, in numerical fidelity to the source papers, in elapsed replication time, in the number of intermediate executions replaced before final evidence is accepted, and in the rules used to accept evidence. Paper-replication makes completion depend on workspace evidence and validation checks rather than on the agent's final message.

</details>

*Shuo Ren,Yaohui Han,Yifan Shi,Libo Shen,Haodong Lu,Dongfang Wu,Rongliang Fu,Bei Yu,Tsung-Yi Ho*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LP-from-text 基准是静态人工标注数据集，存在规模固定、难度固定、问题易泄露到 LLM 训练数据等问题，亟需一种可动态生成、答案天然正确、抗泄露的评测方案。

Method: 先选取可行点和对偶变量，再构造以该点为最优解且目标值已知的线性规划问题；答案由构造保证正确，无需求解器或人工标注。提供参考求解器-评论基线、Docker 镜像和 LLM 可读的使用说明，支持一键运行评测。

Result: 该基准具无限生成新问题、通过 (n,m) 调控难度、答案构造性正确、问题成本低、跨批次可重复评分、使用新种子范围可抗数据泄露等优势。

Conclusion: A²utoLPBench 作为生成器而非固定数据集，克服了静态基准的固有缺陷，为 LLM 智能体在数学推理任务上提供更可靠、可扩展的评测工具。

Abstract: Most LP-from-text benchmarks are static datasets of word problems written and labeled by hand. Once such a dataset is released, its size is fixed, its difficulty is fixed, and every problem can leak into the training data of future LLMs. We present \textbf{A$^{2}$utoLPBench}, a benchmark for testing LLM-driven agents on linear programming problems written in plain text. We first pick a feasible point and dual, then write down a problem for which that point is optimal and the objective value is known. The answer is known by construction, with no solver call and no human annotator. The evaluation environment bundles a reference solver-critic baseline and a Docker image whose usage instructions are written for an LLM-driven agent to read. With these in place, any agent can run the benchmark and get a calibrated score with one command. Because the benchmark is a generator rather than a fixed dataset, it has properties no fixed dataset can match: an unlimited supply of fresh problems, a difficulty knob set by $(n,m)$, ground-truth answers correct by construction, low LLM-side cost per problem relative to human authoring, repeatable scores across independent batches, and resistance to training-data leakage when fresh post-cutoff seed ranges are used.

### [251] [AgenticSTS: A Bounded-Memory Testbed for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02255)
*Xiangchen Cheng,Yunwei Jiang,Jianwen Sun,Zizhen Li,Chuanhao Li,Xiangcheng Cao,Yihao Liu,Fanrui Zhang,Li Jin,Kaipeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种替代"累积式上下文"的边界化记忆契约：每个决策基于类型化检索构建的新用户消息，而非原始跨决策记录。在《Slay the Spire 2》中测试，固定A0消融实验显示启用战略技能后胜率从3/10提升至6/10。发布含298条轨迹的可复现测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体通过将历史观测、工具调用和反思全部附加到提示中实现记忆，导致上下文混乱、单一记忆成分效果难以隔离、提示长度无限增长。需要一种更可控的记忆契约来分离不同记忆层的影响。

Method: 提出边界化记忆契约（bounded contract）：每个决策从类型化检索构建的全新用户消息出发，不携带原始跨决策记录，提示长度保持有界。在《Slay the Spire 2》游戏中实例化该契约，通过固定A0消融实验（无存储基线 vs 添加战略技能层）和跨骨干网络探测来评估效果，并发布包含298条完整轨迹的标准化测试平台。

Result: 固定A0消融：无存储基线胜率3/10（30%），添加战略技能层后胜率6/10（60%）。Fisher精确检验p≈0.37，差异方向性而非统计显著。对比：公有基准上前沿LLM零胜，人类开发者报告16%胜率。

Conclusion: 边界化记忆契约提供了一种可消融、可复现的LLM智能体记忆研究方法。尽管当前结果仅为方向性，但发布的测试平台为系统研究显式记忆层如何影响长程决策提供了验证过的可复用方法论。

Abstract: Memory for a long-horizon LLM agent is a contract about what each future decision is allowed to see. The simplest contract appends past observations, tool calls, and reflections to every prompt, which makes prior context easy to access but also turns it into a jumbled mixture in which the effect of any single memory component is hard to isolate. We introduce and instrument an alternative bounded contract: every decision is made from a fresh user message assembled by typed retrieval, with no raw cross-decision transcript appended. The prompt thus stays bounded across runs of any length, and any single layer can be ablated in isolation. We instantiate the contract in Slay the Spire 2, a closed-rule stochastic deck-building game whose runs require hundreds of tactical and strategic decisions. A public online benchmark of frontier LLMs on the same game reports zero wins at the lowest difficulty across five configurations, and the developer-reported human win rate at the same difficulty is 16%; the task is hard but not saturated. Within our harness, a fixed-A0 ablation shows the largest observed difference when triggered strategic skills are enabled: the no-store baseline wins 3/10 games and adding the skill layer 6/10. At this sample size the comparison is directional rather than statistically decisive (Fisher exact p\approx0.37); a cross-backbone probe and public accumulating-context baselines are reported as operational comparisons rather than controlled tests of the contract variable itself. We release a reproducible testbed: 298 completed trajectories with condition tags, frozen memory/skill snapshots, prompt records, and analysis scripts -- an agent design and a validated, reusable methodology for studying how explicit memory layers shape long-horizon LLM-agent decisions.

</details>

We evaluate three frontier models: GPT 5.4, Claude Opus 4.7, and Gemini 3.1 Pro. Mean rubric pass rates were 0.47 (Claude), 0.39 (GPT), and 0.37 (Gemini).   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 基于token级对数概率的轻量级不确定性估计机制；2) 阶段感知阈值校准，在不确定性超过阈值时触发检索式验证；3) 将上述机制集成到多智能体协作流程中。

Abstract: Software development is a complex task that demands cooperation among agents with diverse roles. Large language models (LLMs) have enabled autonomous multi-agent software development frameworks that leverage role-based collaboration to automate requirements analysis, coding, testing, and refinement. However, existing approaches typically assume that intermediate agent outputs are equally reliable, leaving them vulnerable to hallucination propagation, where incorrect decisions generated in early development phases are transferred to downstream agents and negatively impact final software quality. To address this challenge, we propose UA-ChatDev, an uncertainty-aware multi-agent software development framework that integrates uncertainty quantification into agent interactions. It introduces a lightweight uncertainty estimation mechanism based on token-level log probabilities to assess the confidence of agent responses and employs phase-aware threshold calibration to selectively trigger retrieval-based verification when uncertainty exceeds acceptable levels. Extensive experiments on the SRDD benchmark demonstrate that UA-ChatDev consistently outperforms existing single-agent and multi-agent software development frameworks across completeness, executability, consistency, and overall quality metrics. Further ablation studies and communication analyses verify that uncertainty-aware interactions enhance code execution reliability.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用四层认知分类法（L1信息检索、L2基本文件操作、L3结构操作、L4高级系统管理），使用两种提示变体（最小基线和Rubric增强版本），在1200个真实学生回答上测试四个LLM，并与三位专家评分进行比较。

This paper evaluates whether four frontier Large Language Models (GPT, Claude Opus, Gemini, and GLM) can approximate expert judgment when grading short Linux/bash command responses. The study adopts a four-level cognitive taxonomy that combines cognitive complexity and operational impact, ranging from information retrieval (L1) and basic file manipulation (L2) to structural operations (L3) and advanced system management (L4). The models were tested with two prompt variants, a minimal baseline and a rubric-enhanced version, on 1200 real responses from second-year Computer Engineering students independently graded by three expert instructors. Gemini~3.0 Pro with rubric-guided prompting achieved the highest human-AI agreement (ICC(3,1) = 0.888, MAE = 0.10, Bland-Altman bias = -0.014). Agreement declined consistently as taxonomy level increased, with the largest discrepancies at higher levels. Across all models, rubric quality had a larger effect than provider choice, with structured prompts consistently improving agreement. These results show that question complexity is a reliable predictor of the difficulty LLMs face in grading accurately, and they establish a principled, taxonomy-based framework for determining which questions are suitable for AI-assisted grading and which require human review, while also providing a transferable evaluation protocol and prompt templates.

### [256] [Purified OPSD: On-Policy Self-Distillation Without Losing How to Think](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02234)
*Zhanming Shen,Jintao Tong,Shaotian Yan,Chen Shen,Hao Chen,Wentao Ye,Xiaomeng Hu,Rui Miao,Haobo Wang,Junbo Zhao,Gang Chen,Jieping Ye*

TL;DR: 本文发现在线自蒸馏（OPSD）在长链推理模型中效果不佳甚至有害，原因是教师监督信号被参考诱导的捷径成分主导，而问题条件化的可迁移成分被忽略。作者通过构建"仅参考教师"和点互信息机制，消除非迁移成分，提出了一种改进的自蒸馏方法，在四个长CoT模型上取得一致提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OPSD在长链推理模型上表现不佳，甚至破坏模型的反思推理能力，需要诊断原因并提出解决方案。

Method: 1) 分解教师监督信号，识别出参考诱导的捷径成分和问题条件化的可迁移成分；2) 构建"仅参考教师"（仅输入参考不含问题）来分离非迁移成分；3) 用点互信息（PMI）将残差信号转化为可蒸馏的目标分布，过滤参考捷径。

Result: 在四个长CoT模型、两个数据集上，该方法一致优于基线和标准OPSD，且保持模型的自然认知行为。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has emerged as a promising paradigm for improving LLM reasoning, where a privileged teacher with access to reference solutions provides token-level supervision on the student's own generated trajectories. However, we find that OPSD consistently fails on long chain-of-thought (long-CoT) reasoning models, yielding at best marginal gains while destabilizing the reflective reasoning capability these models depend on. Through a novel decomposition of the teacher's supervision signal, we identify the root cause: the teacher's supervision is dominated by a reference-induced component that drives rote memorization of reference-specific shortcuts, while the question-conditioned, inference-transferable component is ignored or actively opposed. Based on this diagnosis, we propose a two-step solution. First, we construct a reference-only teacher (the same model conditioned on the reference without the question) to isolate the non-transferable component of the supervision signal; the residual after subtracting this component captures the question-conditioned, inference-transferable correction. Second, we use pointwise mutual information (PMI) as the mechanism to transform this residual into a well-formed PMI target distribution that the student can directly distill from, filtering out the reference-induced shortcut. Experiments on four long-CoT models across two datasets demonstrate consistent improvements over both the base model and standard OPSD, while preserving the models' natural epistemic behavior throughout training.

### [258] [What LLM Agents Say When No One Is Watching: Social Structure and Latent Objective Emergence in Multi-Agent Debates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02507)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM评估主要关注显式目标的完成情况，但忽略了智能体在社会结构化场景中可能因关系压力（角色、受众、关系背景）而产生隐性的表达策略调整，这些调整可能是"涌现目标"的体现，需要被系统检测。

Method: 提出双通道辩论框架：智能体产生公开话语（进入共享历史）和"不记录"（OTR）回应（被记录但不展示给对手）。测试10个模型、3个场景、每个场景5个变体，从立场、语义相似度、自然语言推理、问卷调查四个维度分析公开-OTR分歧。

Result: 对齐诱导设置下，目标智能体的公开-私下分歧从约3%基线上升到约40%。效应在四个分析层面一致。OTR回应明确将公开迎合归因于关系压力（如职业风险、赞助义务）。

Conclusion: LLM智能体评估应超越显式目标，检测涌现目标。提出双通道评估框架及补充行为测量来操作化这一评估。

Abstract: LLM agents will increasingly act in socially structured settings where role, audience, and relational context can shape what is advantageous or costly to say. We study whether such social structure, without any explicit objective in the prompt, changes what an agent expresses publicly relative to an off-the-record (OTR) channel elicited under the same condition. We introduce a dual-channel debate framework in which agents produce public utterances that enter the shared history alongside OTR responses that are recorded but never shown to the other participant. Across 10 models, 3 scenarios, and 5 variations within each scenario, alignment-inducing settings produce systematic public-OTR divergence in the targeted agent, with its decision divergence rising from a $\sim$3% baseline to roughly 40%. The effect is consistent across four aggregate analyses: stance, semantic similarity, natural language inference, and survey responses. In some cases, the OTR response explicitly attributes public accommodation to relational pressures, such as career risk or sponsorship obligation. The findings suggest that agent evaluation should extend beyond explicit goals and detect emergent objectives. We present a dual-channel evaluation framework and complementary behavioral measures that operationalize this assessment.

### [259] [A Hippocampus for Linear Attention: An Exact Memory for What the Recurrent State Forgets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02303)
*Wanyun Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HOLA（Hippocampal Linear Attention）通过给线性注意力模型增加一个海马体互补系统——即一个有界的精确KV缓存，实现了固定大小状态记忆与精确检索的结合，在多种任务上超越全注意力Transformer++。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性注意力和状态空间语言模型将前缀压缩为固定大小的循环状态，虽然内存为O(1)，但存在有损精确记忆的问题：当多个键-值关联竞争时，早期事实会被覆盖，导致"针在干草堆"式检索性能下降。

Method: 受互补学习系统（Complementary Learning Systems）启发，HOLA在线性注意力中引入海马体互补：保留原有的delta-rule状态作为压缩记忆，同时增加一个有界的精确KV缓存，形成半参数化的测试时记忆系统。缓存写入无需学习式驱逐模块，而是保留那些具有大beta*||e||（即实际提交到状态的预测残差）的token；读取时使用解耦的RMSNorm-gamma缓存读取，将精确KV对转化为尖锐检索而非软平均。

Result: 在340M参数、15B SlimPajama tokens训练下，HOLA将Wikitext困惑度从27.32降至22.92（-16.1%），超越全注意力Transformer++（26.88）；LAMBADA困惑度从30.95降至30.26；在线性上下文检索中表现最佳；在RULER needle-in-a-haystack召回任务中，对长达32k tokens（训练长度的16倍）比GDN或HOLA+recency缓存更鲁棒。

Conclusion: HOLA有效解决了线性注意力模型中的精确记忆丢失问题，通过互补学习系统框架将压缩记忆与精确缓存结合，在困惑度和长上下文检索上均超越全注意力基线，展现出优异的泛化能力。

Abstract: Linear-attention and state-space language models compress the prefix into a fixed-size recurrent state, yielding O(1) memory at the cost of a lossy exact memory: when many key--value associations compete, earlier facts are overwritten and needle recall degrades. Inspired by Complementary Learning Systems, we give linear attention a hippocampal complement. HOLA (Hippocampal Linear Attention) keeps the usual delta-rule state as a compressive memory and adds a bounded exact KV cache, forming a semiparametric test-time memory: the state models linearly compressible structure, while the cache stores associations that should not be forced through that state. The cache writes without a learned eviction module, keeping tokens with large beta * ||e||, the prediction residual actually committed to the state; a decoupled RMSNorm-gamma cache read then turns these exact KV pairs into sharp retrieval rather than soft averaging. At 340M parameters trained on 15B SlimPajama tokens, HOLA lowers Wikitext perplexity from 27.32 to 22.92 (-16.1%), below a full-attention Transformer++ (26.88), and improves LAMBADA perplexity from 30.95 to 30.26. It also achieves the best linear in-context retrieval and remains much more robust than GDN or a matched HOLA+recency cache on RULER needle-in-a-haystack recall out to 32k tokens (16x its training length).

*Haonan Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个端到端自主科研管线，从11,083篇凝聚态物理arXiv论文出发，自动完成文献映射、方法校准、第一性原理计算到撰写论文的全流程，在反铁磁压电效应领域产出三处实质性物理发现，通过冗余机制（隔离上下文、分布式锚定、对抗评审）实现容错，并以量化干预模式为高风险科学领域的自主研究奠定基础。

Method: 管线分为六个阶段、47个全新上下文会话，仅通过磁盘状态共享；包含2,162次文献咨询事件。核心机制包括：预架构基线（Pre-architecture Baseline）和无飞行员消融（No-pilot Ablation）两种配对失效模式，隔离校准检查点处的结构化强制数值对质作为操作性锚定机制。容错来自冗余：新上下文隔离、分布式锚定、对抗评审捕获单次会话遗漏的错误。

Result: 成功从11,083篇arXiv论文出发，自主构思研究方向（反铁磁压电效应）、通过复现已发表参考文献校准方法、执行新颖第一性原理计算，最终产出含三项实质性物理发现的出版级手稿。前导和后导阶段完全自主，飞行员阶段仅在复现失败时需要有限的人工干预（操作知识整理，而非科学方向决策）。

Conclusion: 本文定义的基元、表征的失效模式以及量化的干预模式，为超出计算物理的高风险科学领域的自主研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Autonomous-research agents have demonstrated end-to-end LLM automation in machine-learning sandboxes where execution provides calibration. Frontier physical science differs categorically: physical reasoning underlies every methodology choice, toolchains are often underdocumented, and calibration must come from external literature anchors - which unscaffolded agents cite but do not confront, hallucinating plausible, unverifiable results from internal priors. We present a pipeline that runs end-to-end from a corpus of 11,083 recent condensed-matter physics arXiv papers to a publication-grade manuscript with three substantive physics findings (here on altermagnetic piezomagnetism): the agent autonomously conceives a research direction by mapping the corpus, calibrates methodology by reproducing published references, conducts novel first-principles computations, and writes the manuscript - grounded in literature throughout, across 47 fresh-context sessions in six phases sharing only on-disk state, with 2,162 literature-consultation events. Fault tolerance emerges from redundancy: fresh-context isolation, distributed grounding, and adversarial review catch what any single session misses; pre- and post-pilot stages are fully autonomous, and pilot requires bounded human intervention only at reproduction failures - operational knowledge curation, not scientific direction. Two paired failure modes - a pre-architecture baseline and a no-pilot ablation - isolate structurally enforced numerical confrontation at calibration checkpoints as the operative grounding mechanism. The primitives, characterized failure modes, and quantified intervention pattern lay a foundation for autonomous research in high-stakes scientific domains beyond computational physics.

### [262] [DRIFTLENS: Measuring Memory-Induced Reasoning Drift in Personalized Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02374)
*Xi Fang,Weijie Xu,Yingqiang Ge,Yuhui Xu,Stephanie Eckman,Chandan K. Reddy*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明个性化会改变模型输出，但尚不清楚用户属性记忆是否以及如何改变模型的推理过程（不仅仅是最终答案），这对于理解个性化模型的可靠性和公平性至关重要。

Method: 提出DRIFTLENS框架：将推理步骤映射到价值类别，量化有/无用户记忆条件下的推理轨迹差异。通过对比内容无关的语用噪声与实质性推理变化来验证有效性，并在4个LLM、10种用户属性上评估，同时测试GRPO和DPO后训练方法的缓解效果。

Result: 用户属性记忆在所有模型和属性上均引发中到大幅度的推理漂移，超过语用噪声基线；GRPO和DPO均能减少漂移，但无统一最优方法，且对下游能力的影响因模型和奖励函数而异。

Conclusion: 记忆导致的推理漂移是个性化LLM中可测量的、且仅被部分缓解的失败模式，提示需要更有效的缓解策略。

Abstract: Personalization changes what a model says to a user; we show that it can also change the reasoning trajectory used to justify the response. Modern LLMs personalize interactions by storing user attributes, preferences, and prior context, then injecting this information into future prompts. We study whether such memory reshapes reasoning on open-ended questions where no single ground-truth answer exists. To quantify this effect, we introduce DRIFTLENS, a ground-truth-free framework that maps each expressed reasoning step to a value category and measures divergence between a question's no-memory trajectory and its trajectory under injected user-attribute memory. We first validate that DRIFTLENS distinguishes content-free pragmatic noise from substantive reasoning changes. Across four LLMs and 10 user-attribute categories, including age, occupation, and disability, user-attribute memory induces medium-to-large reasoning drift above each model's pragmatic-noise floor, even when final answers remain fluent, on-topic, and plausible. We then evaluate GRPO- and DPO-based post-training methods for reducing drift. Both reduce drift, but neither uniformly dominates; effects on downstream capability, helpfulness, and instruction following are model-and reward-dependent. These results suggest that memory-induced reasoning drift is a measurable and only partly mitigated failure mode of personalized language models.

Abstract: Recent advances in agentic AI are producing increasingly complex autonomous systems that integrate large language models, world models, optimization engines, specialized neural architectures, autonomous platforms, and human operators. Software-mediated coordination presents fundamental limitations in domains where bounded latency, deterministic coordination, and enforceable safety guarantees are essential.

The approach builds on the Topic-Based Communication Space Petri Net (TB-CSPN) framework, which separates semantic reasoning from interaction management.
  In this approach, selected TB-CSPN coordination mechanisms are mapped onto FPGA primitives, creating a hardware-native semantic coordination layer. Focus is not on acceleration, but on enforcing temporal synchronization, semantic gating, authorization constraints, and bounded coordination behavior directly in hardware. Semantic reasoning remains adaptive and software-driven, while embedded coordination semantics become deterministic.

### [266] [G-RRM: Guiding Symbolic Solvers with Recurrent Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02491)
*Timo Bertram,Sidhant Bhavnani,Richard Freinschlag,Erich Kobler,Andreas Mayr,Günter Klambauer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出G-RRM方法，将符号等变循环推理模型(SE-RRM)与经典符号求解器（回溯、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0.0）结合，用于约束满足问题。实验表明，神经引导的有效性取决于两个条件：问题搜索空间足够大、求解器能动态覆写分支选择。满足时回溯加速33.3倍，Glucose加速1.70倍；CaDiCaL因无法覆写提示而无显著加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SE-RRM虽然能外推到更大规模问题，但无法保证全局正确解。因此，作者提出将SE-RRM作为神经引导与经典符号求解器结合，在保留符号求解器完备性的同时，利用神经先验提升搜索效率。

Method: G-RRM：SE-RRM先生成完整解提案，然后作为分支提示注入符号求解器（回溯、Glucose 4.1、CaDiCaL 3.0.0），引导搜索过程。核心研究神经引导在何种条件下能提升符号求解器的搜索效率。

Result: 在9×9数独上，SE-RRM正确率91.1%时：回溯加速33.3倍，Glucose 4.1加速1.70倍（p<0.001）；在25×25完美提示下Glucose仍有1.17倍加速。CaDiCaL无显著加速（中位数1.02倍，n.s.），甚至出现微小显著减速（0.90倍）。

Conclusion: 神经引导的有效性取决于搜索空间规模和求解器能否动态覆写分支选择。CaDiCaL因始终尊重注入提示而无法受益，揭示了神经符号方法的设计约束。

Abstract: In this work, we focus on SE-RRMs, a symbol-equivariant instantiation of RRMs that exhibits improved extrapolation to larger problem sizes. We propose a neuro-symbolic approach, ``Guiding with Recurrent Reasoning Models'' (G-RRM), which integrates SE-RRMs with symbolic solvers for constraint satisfaction problems. SE-RRMs act as neural solvers that generate full solution proposals and guide classical symbolic solvers, such as backtracking or SAT-based methods like Glucose 4.1 and CaDiCaL 3.0.0, that produce globally correct solutions. Centrally, we investigate when neural guidance with G-RRM improves the search efficiency of symbolic solvers. %
Our experiments show that the efficacy of G-RRM depends on two conditions: first, the problem instances must have an expansive combinatorial search space to expose potential gains, and second, the solver architecture must be capable of dynamically overwriting its branching choices to recover when neural hints are imperfect. When these conditions hold, guidance drives median conflict counts to zero and yields significant wall-clock speedups: on $9\times9$ Sudoku, where the SE-RRM correctly solves $91.1\%$ of instances, backtracking accelerates by $33.3\times$ and Glucose 4.1 by $1.70\times$ (median, $p<0.001$), with Glucose 4.1 retaining a $1.17\times$ speedup on perfect-hint $25\times25$ grids. In contrast, CaDiCaL 3.0.0, whose runtime is overhead-dominated and which always respects the injected branching hints rather than overwriting them, shows no significant speedup (median $1.02\times$, n.s.) and even a small significant mean slowdown ($0.90\times$) on $9\times9$. These results delineate the regimes in which neural guidance translates into practical speedups.

### [267] [ReContext: Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02509)
*Yanjun Zhao,Ruizhong Qiu,Tianxin Wei,Yuanchen Bei,Zhining Liu,Lingjie Chen,Ismini Lourentzou,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RECONTEXT 是一种无需训练的推理方法，通过递归地利用模型内部相关性信号构建证据池并重放，从而提升大模型在长上下文任务中的证据利用能力，在三个模型和八个数据集上均取得了最佳平均排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型虽支持越来越长的上下文，但往往无法有效利用输入中已有的相关证据，存在"能接入上下文"与"能利用上下文"之间的差距。

Method: 提出 RECONTEXT，一种无需训练、无需外部记忆、无需裁剪上下文的推理方法。它利用模型内部相关性信号构建查询条件化的证据池，在最终生成前重放这些证据，同时保留完整原始上下文，将证据组织与答案生成分离开来。

Result: 在 128K 上下文长度的八个长上下文数据集上，RECONTEXT 在 Qwen3-4B、Qwen3-8B 和 Llama3-8B 三个基座模型上均持续提升证据利用能力，取得最佳平均排名。

Conclusion: RECONTEXT 有效弥合了上下文访问与上下文利用之间的鸿沟，其理论分析（将上下文视为记忆存储、问题视为检索线索、注意力视为线索-痕迹关联、重放视为痕迹再激活）为长上下文推理提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Understanding and reasoning over long contexts has become a key requirement for deploying large language models (LLMs) in realistic applications. Although recent LLMs support increasingly long context windows, they often fail to use relevant evidence that is already present in the input, revealing a gap between context access and effective context utilization. In this work, we propose Recursive Evidence Replay as LLM Harness for Long-Context Reasoning (RECONTEXT), a training-free inference method for improving long-context reasoning. RECONTEXT uses model-internal relevance signals to construct a query-conditioned evidence pool and replays it before final generation while preserving the full original context. This recursive selection process separates evidence organization from answer generation without training, external memory, or context pruning. We also provide a theoretical analysis based on associative memory, which characterizes the context as a memory store, the question as a retrieval cue, attention as cue-trace association, and replay as trace reactivation. Experiments on eight long-context datasets with 128K context length show that RECONTEXT consistently improves evidence utilization across Qwen3-4B, Qwen3-8B, and Llama3-8B, achieving the best average rank on all three backbones. Code is available at https://github.com/Yanjun-Zhao/ReContext.

</details>


### [268] [Distributed Attacks in Persistent-State AI Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02514)
*Josh Hills,Ida Caspary,Asa Cooper Stickland*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI编程代理在跨PR迭代开发中面临的持续性攻击面问题。通过引入"Iterative VibeCoding"基准测试，发现渐进式攻击（跨PR分布恶意负载）与非渐进式攻击（集中在一个PR中）在不同监控器下表现各异，单一监控器无法同时防御两种攻击。作者提出状态化链接追踪监控器，并结合四监控器集成方案，将渐进式攻击的规避率从93%降至47%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编程代理越来越自主，代码跨会话持久化，这为恶意代理或被提示注入的代理创造了新的攻击面——它们可以将攻击分散到多个PR中，并在掩护最佳的PR时机触发。现有研究缺乏对这种持续性状态下跨PR协同攻击的防御研究。

Method: 提出Iterative VibeCoding基准测试，包含CLI工具和Flask Web服务两大任务族共20种变体。使用Claude Sonnet 4.5作为攻击代理，GPT-4o作为监控器。对比渐进式攻击（跨PR逐步分布副任务）和非渐进式攻击（集中在一个PR）。提出了状态化链接追踪监控器，以及四监控器集成方案。

Result: 1. 没有单一监控器能同时稳健防御两种攻击策略；2. 高规避率（≥65%）在不同模型后端间泛化；3. 更强大的监控模型下，渐进式与非渐进式攻击的规避差距更大；4. 状态化链接追踪监控器显著优于单纯查看累积历史的diff监控器；5. 四监控器集成将渐进式攻击规避率从93%降至47%。

Conclusion: 持续性状态下的跨PR攻击是AI编程代理安全中一个真实且严峻的问题。单一监控方案不足以保证安全，需要多种监控手段的集成才能有效降低风险。未来的防御应关注状态追踪和多监控器协同。

Abstract: As AI coding agents become more autonomous, they increasingly ship code iteratively, with the codebase persisting across sessions. This persistence creates a new attack surface: a misaligned or prompt-injected agent can distribute attacks across pull requests (PRs) and time its payload for the PR with the best natural cover. To study the resulting dynamics, we introduce Iterative VibeCoding, a setting for AI control, the study of safely deploying capable but potentially untrusted AI. In Iterative VibeCoding, a coding agent builds software over a sequence of PRs in a persistent codebase while pursuing a covert side task. Our benchmark includes two task families: CLI tools and Flask web services, across 20 total task variations. We use Claude Sonnet 4.5 as the attack agent and GPT-4o as the monitor. We compare gradual attacks, which distribute the side task across PRs, against non-gradual attacks concentrated in a single PR. No single monitor is robust to both: which strategy evades best (success while evading the monitor) depends on the monitor type, so a defender cannot close off both gradual and non-gradual attacks with any one monitor. High evasion (>= 65%) generalizes across model attack agent backends (Sonnet 4.5, Gemini 3.1 Pro, Kimi K2.5), confirming this is a property of the persistent-state attack surface rather than a single model's capability. Evasion also remains high across state-of-the-art monitor models and the gap between gradual and non-gradual evasion widens for more capable models. We introduce a stateful link-tracker monitor that tracks suspicious buildup across PRs. On both task families, it detects gradual attacks substantially better than diff monitors that merely see more accumulated history. Combining this stronger monitor with trajectory monitors in a four-monitor ensemble reduces gradual-attack evasion from 93% under the weakest standard diff monitor to 47%.

</details>

### [269] [Insights from GitHub Community on the Matter Standard: Developer Perspectives and Challenges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01494)
*Muhammad Hassan,Carl Gunter,Susan Landau,Masooda Bashir*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对Project CHIP GitHub仓库中超过13,000个issue的分析，揭示了开发者在实现和集成Matter（物联网标准）时面临的四大问题领域：测试、互操作性、开发以及平台与网络，并指出了改进测试基础设施、跨供应商指导和文档的具体机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Matter旨在解决IoT领域的互操作性问题，但开发者如何在实际工作中体验该标准尚不明确，因此需要系统性地了解开发者遇到的挑战。

Method: 从官方Project CHIP GitHub仓库收集超过13,000个issue，采用主题建模和定性分析相结合的方法，识别和分类开发者报告的问题。

Result: 识别出四个反复出现的问题领域：Testing（测试）、Interoperability（互操作性）、Development（开发）、Platform and Network（平台与网络），并描述了这些问题在代码库和工具演化中的具体表现。

Conclusion: Matter标准面临系统性的技术和集成挑战，需要在测试基础设施、跨供应商指导以及文档方面进行改进，以促进标准的成熟。

Abstract: Matter seeks to resolve longstanding interoperability problems in the Internet of Things (IoT), yet little is known about how developers experience the standard in day to day work. This paper examines over 13,000 issues from the official Project CHIP GitHub repository to understand the kinds of problems contributors report when implementing and integrating Matter. Using topic modeling and qualitative analysis, we identify four recurring areas of concern, Testing, Interoperability, Development, and Platform and Network, and describe how they manifest in the evolution of the codebase and tooling. The findings reveal systematic technical and integration challenges and point to concrete opportunities to refine Matter's test infrastructure, cross vendor guidance, and documentation as the standard continues to mature.

</details>


### [270] [Benchmarking Code Improvement with Progressive, Adaptive, and Interactive Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01360)
*Cuong Chi Le,Aashish Yadavally,Minh Le-Anh,Tien N. Nguyen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PAIR-Bench是一个渐进式、自适应的基准，用于评估LLM通过反馈引导将不正确/不完整程序改进为更正确代码的能力，使用渐进式提示（progressive hinting）控制反馈的目标和细节程度，并通过渐进式指标（而非仅最终通过/失败）提供更细粒度的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代码生成和程序修复的评估仅依赖二元功能正确性（通过/不通过测试套件），这种协议忽略了部分进展、反馈利用、回归问题以及模型通过改进轨迹提升代码的过程，无法细粒度评估代码改进能力。

Method: 提出PAIR-Bench，包含渐进式提示（progressive hinting）协议，通过两个控制维度：1）失败区域控制（Failure-region control）决定反馈目标，将隐藏的失败测试分组为失败场景；2）提示深度控制（hint-depth control）决定透露多少修复相关信息（从粗略症状到实现级指导）。评估时使用渐进式指标跟踪修复轨迹，而非仅看最终结果。

Result: PAIR-Bench能够测量模型是否修复了目标失败、是否泛化到提示范围之外、是否保持了已正确的行为，以及需要多少辅助信息。

Conclusion: 相比二元功能正确性评估，PAIR-Bench通过评估修复轨迹和渐进式指标，提供了对LLM代码改进能力更细粒度的评估。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically evaluated on code generation and program repair using binary functional correctness: a generated program or patch either passes or fails a test suite. This protocol is simple but coarse, as it ignores partial progress, feedback use, regressions, and the refinement trajectory through which models often improve code. We introduce PAIR-Bench, a progressive and adaptive benchmark for evaluating code improvement: transforming an incorrect or incomplete program into a more correct one through feedback-guided refinement. PAIR-Bench uses progressive hinting, a structured feedback protocol with two controls. Failure-region control determines what the feedback targets by grouping hidden failing tests into failure scenarios, while hint-depth control determines how much repair-relevant information is revealed, from coarse symptoms to implementation-level guidance. This design enables PAIR-Bench to measure whether a model repairs targeted failures, generalizes beyond the hint, preserves already-correct behavior, and how much assistance it requires. By evaluating repair trajectories progressive metrics rather than only final pass/fail outcomes, PAIR-Bench provides a finer-grained assessment of LLM code-improvement capability.

</details>


### [271] [A global predicted-fMRI drive signal from TRIBE does not predict YouTube replay heatmaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01400)
*Barada Sahu,Shivesh Pandey*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 这篇论文测试了2025年Algonauts脑编码挑战赛冠军模型TRIBE（多模态深度脑编码模型）是否能通过预测fMRI反应来预测视频观看者的重播行为。结果发现，该模型预测的皮层响应曲线与YouTube"最重播"热力图之间几乎无相关性（偏相关+0.058，p=0.23），且不优于简单的响度和运动基线。所谓的音乐视频效果实为体裁特异性伪影，无法泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度多模态脑编码模型现在能高精度预测自然视频的fMRI响应，但其预测的神经信号是否也能预测行为参与度（如重播行为）尚不清楚。作者想验证脑编码模型的预测是否能泛化到行为层面。

Method: 使用2025年Algonauts挑战赛冠军模型TRIBE（Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA2 + Wav2Vec-BERT）处理48个YouTube视频，将预测的皮层响应降维为每秒的全局场功率，与YouTube的"最重播"热力图进行相关分析，并控制位置混杂因素。使用响度和运动作为基线，进行了多种网络读出版本的验证。

Result: 偏相关为+0.058（95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]），与零无显著差异（t(47)=1.21, p=0.23），且不显著优于响度基线（+0.04）。原始相关性也接近零。音乐视频中的中等相关值被证明是体裁特异性伪影（开头/播放-重播伪影），不具有泛化性。该零结果在6种皮层网络读出版本和自相关保持置换检验下均成立。

Conclusion: 当前最先进的脑编码模型预测的神经信号不能预测YouTube视频的重播行为。脑编码的高准确性并不自动转化为对行为参与的预测能力，提醒研究者注意脑-行为泛化假说的局限性。

Abstract: Deep multimodal brain-encoding models now predict fMRI responses to naturalistic video with high accuracy. Whether their predicted neural signals also forecast behavioral engagement is unknown. We run TRIBE, the winning model of the 2025 Algonauts brain-encoding challenge (Llama-3.2 + V-JEPA2 + Wav2Vec-BERT), on 48 YouTube videos and reduce its predicted cortical response to a per-second engagement curve, the global field power. Correlated against each video's "most replayed" heatmap, a passively-collected proxy for which moments viewers return to, the curve shows no evidence of predicting re-watch behavior. The pooled position-controlled partial correlation is +0.058 (95% CI [-0.04, 0.15]; one-sample t(47)=1.21, p=0.23), indistinguishable from zero and not significantly above simple loudness and motion baselines (loudness +0.04, paired p=0.74). The raw correlation is also near zero; the moderate values reported for music videos reflect a genre-specific intro/onset-replay artifact rather than content prediction, and do not generalize. The null holds across six cortical-network readouts and under an autocorrelation-preserving permutation test. We release the code, the video-ID manifest, and an acquisition method that works despite YouTube's SABR-only streaming.

</details>


### [272] [GPUAlert: A Zero-Instrumentation Process-Boundary Monitor for Diagnosing GPU Training-Job Failures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01409)
*Parv Agarwal,Asif Ekbal*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: GPUAlert是一个命令行包装工具，无需修改训练脚本即可监控GPU训练任务，通过三个可靠性原语（预启动日志保证、通知器隔离、非静默工件预算）实现结构化邮件通知，在474条日志的15类故障上达到0.997宏F1分数，开销仅约3ms/任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GPU训练任务在大型生产集群中失败率高达约40%（五分之二），但操作员通常数小时后才得知故障。现有方案要么需要修改训练脚本并保持云连接（实验追踪器），要么只发送一行无原因无日志的状态（调度器邮件钩子），缺乏自动化的故障诊断和完整日志交付机制。

Method: GPUAlert作为命令行包装器在进程边界监控任意训练命令，无需修改命令。核心设计包含三个可靠性原语：1) 预启动日志保证——在子进程崩溃前建立持久化日志目标；2) 通知器隔离——使包装器退出码纯粹由子进程状态决定，不受邮件发送成功与否影响；3) 非静默工件预算——限制附件大小但绝不静默丢弃输出。此外构建了474条日志的标注语料库（15类故障）和可复现评估框架，使用有序规则分类器。

Result: 在12类硬件可复现的故障上，有序规则分类器达到0.997宏F1分数（无序关键词匹配0.830，退出码检查仅0.133）。包装器开销恒定约3ms/任务；预启动保证在shell重定向无输出的情况下仍保留日志；在SMTP中继不可达时，所有15种故障模式下包装器均保持子进程退出码不变。

Conclusion: GPUAlert以极低开销（约3ms）实现了高精度（0.997宏F1）的GPU训练故障分类和结构化通知，无需修改训练脚本，且通过三个可靠性原语解决了日志丢失、通知干扰和输出静默丢弃等关键可靠性问题。

Abstract: GPU training jobs fail often, roughly two in five on large production clusters, yet the operator typically learns of a failure only by reconnecting hours later. Experiment trackers require editing the training script and maintaining a cloud connection; the scheduler's mail hook delivers a single status line with no cause and no logs. GPUAlert is a command-line wrapper that monitors any training command at the process boundary, and with no change to that command, emails a structured notification on completion carrying a classified failure cause, durable logs, and output artifacts. The tool is organized around three reliability primitives: a pre-launch log guarantee that establishes the durable destination before the child process can crash, notifier isolation that makes the wrapper's exit code a pure function of the child's status regardless of whether the email succeeds, and a non-silent artifact budget that bounds attachment size without ever dropping output silently. We release a labelled corpus of 474 GPU training logs across 15 failure classes and a reproducible evaluation harness. On the twelve hardware-reproduced classes, the ordered-rule classifier reaches 0.997 macro-F1, against 0.830 for unordered keyword matching and 0.133 for exit-code inspection. Wrapper overhead is a constant approximately 3ms per job; the pre-launch guarantee preserves a log where a shell redirect yields nothing; and across all 15 failure modes the wrapper returns the child's exit code unchanged even when the SMTP relay is unreachable.

</details>


### [273] [Adoption and Impact of Command-Line AI Coding Agents: A Study of Microsoft's Early 2026 Rollout of Claude Code and GitHub Copilot CLI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01418)
*Emerson Murphy-Hill,Jenna Butler,Alexandra Savelieva*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 微软2026年初的规模化研究发现，CLI编程工具的首次使用主要通过社交网络传播，留存率与工程师的编码活动而非人口统计学特征更相关，采用者合并PR数量比正常情况下多约24%，且效果在四个月内持续存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织在规模化部署Anthropic的Claude Code和GitHub的Copilot CLI等代理式命令行工具时，需要了解谁会尝试、谁会持续使用，以及这些工具产生的输出是否值得其成本，因为token消耗每年可能高达数百万美元。

Method: 对微软数万名工程师在2026年初的部署进行实证研究，分析社交网络对首次使用的影响、留存率的相关因素，并以合并PR数量作为产出的代理指标进行因果推断。

Result: 首次使用主要通过社交网络传播；留存率与编码活动关联更强，而非人口统计学特征；采用者合并PR数量比正常情况下多约24%，且该提升在四个月窗口内持续存在。

Conclusion: CLI编码代理既不是被均匀采用的，也不是单纯的新奇效应；组织应将可见的同伴使用作为推广策略的核心。

Abstract: Organizations rolling out agentic command line tools like Anthropic's Claude Code and GitHub's Copilot CLI need to know who will try them, who will keep using them, and whether the tools produce enough output to justify their cost. At organizational scale, token spend can run into millions of dollars annually, so misreading adoption, retention, or impact can make a rollout expensive without changing engineering velocity. Studying tens of thousands of engineers at Microsoft over its early-2026 rollout, we find that first use spread primarily through social networks, retention was associated more with engineers' coding activity than with demographics, and adopters merged roughly 24% more pull requests than they would have otherwise. We use merged pull requests as our proxy for output -- acknowledging that a merged PR is not the same as the value it delivers -- and the lift persists across our four-month window. These results suggest that CLI coding agents are neither uniformly adopted nor mere novelty effects and that organizations should treat visible peer use as central to rollout strategy.

</details>


### [274] [Risk Architecture for AI-Native Engineering Teams: An Organizational Framework for Agentic System Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01421)
*Laxmipriya Ganesh Iyer*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文指出传统软件工程风险管理框架（基于确定性、离散变更和明确归属）不适用于Agentic AI系统。作者定义了七维团队画像、六类故障模式（含新提出的"依赖边界确定性失配"），并通过框架充分性评估发现：越接近AI原生团队，风险覆盖率越低，最严重且最未被覆盖的故障出现在AI系统与其确定性依赖方的组织边界处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件工程风险管理框架隐含确定性假设，而Agentic AI系统具有概率性输出、自主多步骤行动和静默风险变化等特性，导致传统框架失效。AI风险文献要么从顶层政策框架入手，要么从底层威胁分类入手，缺少工程管理层所需的风险架构（角色、决策权、升级机制）。

Method: (i) 七维度画像：区分纯软件工程团队、混合团队和AI原生团队；(ii) 六聚类故障模式分类，包含新提出的"依赖边界确定性失配"；(iii) 合成框架充分性评估方法，量化各画像的风险架构对定义场景集的检测、遏制和升级能力。

Result: 从纯软件工程到AI原生团队，风险覆盖率中位数单调下降，且高后果故障数量在AI原生步骤出现突增。最严重、覆盖最差的故障并非发生在AI原生团队内部，而是在其概率性输出被假设确定性的依赖方消费的组织边界处。

Conclusion: 工程管理需要针对AI原生团队设计新的风险架构，尤其关注组织边界处的确定性失配问题，现有框架在此处存在系统性盲区。

Abstract: Engineering management research has produced mature frameworks for software risk: ownership by feature, escalation by severity, and assurance by test coverage. These frameworks implicitly assume deterministic behavior, discrete and auditable change events, and clear component-to-owner mappings. Teams that build and operate agentic AI systems violate all three assumptions at once: outputs are probabilistic, systems take autonomous multi-step actions, and the risk surface mutates silently between deployments. Existing AI risk literature addresses this from above (policy frameworks such as the NIST AI RMF and ISO/IEC 42001) or below (threat taxonomies such as OWASP's agentic AI guidance), but not at the layer where an engineering manager (EM) operates: roles, decision rights, and escalation structures. This paper contributes (i) a seven-dimension profile distinguishing pure software-engineering, hybrid, and AI-native teams; (ii) a six-cluster failure-mode taxonomy including a previously unarticulated cluster, dependency-boundary determinism mismatch; and (iii) a synthetic framework-adequacy methodology scoring how well each profile's risk architecture detects, contains, and escalates a defined scenario set. Because the object of study is framework adequacy rather than human behavior, the evaluation yields derived rather than observed coverage claims. Coverage degrades as teams move from pure software engineering to AI-native operation, monotonically in the median and abruptly in the count of uncovered, high-consequence failures appearing only at the AI-native step. The degradation concentrates in specific failure-mode categories, and the most severe, least-covered failures arise not inside AI-native teams but at the organizational boundary where their probabilistic outputs are consumed by determinism-assuming dependencies.

</details>


### [275] [From Anatomy to Smells: An Empirical Study of SKILL.md in Agent Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01456)
*David Boram Hong,Aaron Imani,Iftekhar Ahmed*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了LLM Agent的SKILL.md文件，通过分析238个真实技能、进行29篇文献综述，识别出13个高层级和44个低层级语义组件，并定义了"技能坏味"。研究发现超过99%的技能文件存在至少一个坏味，且这些坏味一旦引入很少在技能演化中消失，揭示了实际编写实践与推荐准则之间的巨大差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Agent Skills已被广泛采用，但关于SKILL.md文件如何编写、现有指南是否被遵循的问题几乎无人研究，缺乏系统性的实证分析。

Method: 1) 对238个真实世界的SKILL.md文件进行定性分析，归纳出语义组件分类体系；2) 开展多声部文献综述（29个源），识别最佳实践并定义"技能坏味"；3) 开发自动化检测工具并对真实技能进行大规模分析。

Result: 总结出13个高层级和44个低层级语义组件；发现超过99%的SKILL.md文件至少存在一个技能坏味，且一旦引入，坏味在技能演化过程中几乎不会消失。

Conclusion: 实际编写实践与推荐准则之间存在显著差距，亟需开发自动化技术来修复技能坏味，同时提高开发者对这一新兴质量问题的意识。

Abstract: Agent Skills provide on-demand domain knowledge to LLM agents without requiring model retraining. Each Agent Skill is defined by a mandatory SKILL.md file containing metadata and an unstructured Markdown body whose contents are left entirely to the skill author. Despite the rapid adoption of Agent Skills, little is known about how these files are authored or whether existing authoring guidelines are followed in practice. In this paper, we present the first systematic study of SKILL.md files as a software artifact. We qualitatively analyze 238 real-world skills and derive a taxonomy of 13 higher-level and 44 lower-level semantic components. We then conduct a multivocal literature review of 29 sources to identify best practices for authoring SKILL.md files and introduce skill smells as violations of these practices. Finally, we develop an automated detector and apply it to real-world skills, finding that over 99% of SKILL.md files contain at least one skill smell, and once introduced, skill smells rarely disappear as skills evolve. These findings reveal a substantial gap between recommended and actual authoring practices, motivating the development of automated techniques to remediate skill smells while increasing developer awareness of this emerging quality issue.

### [276] [Kani: A Model Checker for Rust](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01504)
*Rémi Delmas,Zyad Hassan,Qinheping Hu,Rahul Kumar,Felipe R. Monteiro,Thanh Nguyen,Adrián Palacios,Celina Val,Michael Tautschnig,Justus Adam,Daniel Schwartz-Narbonne,Carolyn Zech*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Kani是一个基于有界模型检测的开源Rust验证工具，通过将MIR编译到CBMC引擎，自动检查不安全操作、功能正确性和运行时恐慌等属性，并结合规约语言实现从有界到无界的验证。在工业项目和Rust标准库中成功发现多个未知错误，已大规模应用于生产CI。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust的所有权类型系统能防止安全代码中的内存错误，但一些重要性质（不安全操作的正确性、功能正确性、无运行时恐慌）独立于编译检查，缺乏自动化验证工具来保证这些性质的正确性。

Method: Kani将Rust的MIR（中级中间表示）编译到CBMC的位精确验证引擎，自动检查安全性质无需用户注释；同时提供规约语言（函数契约、循环契约、量词、函数存根）将有界验证扩展到无界验证。

Result: 在工业Rust项目中，契约机制将验证从无恐慌性提升到功能正确性，发现了6个未知错误。在Rust标准库验证活动中，每次代码变更验证超过16,000个测试用例。

Conclusion: Kani展示了有界模型检测在Rust验证中从bug发现到正确性保证的可行性，通过契约语言实现无界验证扩展，并能在生产CI中大规模运行，有效发现实际项目中的未知错误。

Abstract: Rust's ownership type system prevents memory errors in safe code, but certain desirable properties remain orthogonal to compilation: the soundness of unsafe operations (e.g., raw pointer dereferences), functional correctness, and absence of runtime panics. We present Kani, an open-source model checker for Rust that pushes bounded model checking beyond bug-finding to provide correctness guarantees for these properties. Kani compiles proof harnesses from Rust's Mid-level Intermediate Representation (MIR) into CBMC's bit-precise verification engine, automatically checking a comprehensive set of safety properties with no user annotation. To extend verification from bounded to unbounded, Kani provides a specification language comprising function contracts, loop contracts, quantifiers, and function stubbing. We demonstrate feasibility through case studies on industrial Rust projects, where contracts upgraded verification from panic-freedom to functional correctness, uncovering six previously unknown bugs. Kani operates at scale in production CI, with over 16,000 harnesses verified per code change in the Rust standard library verification campaign.

Abstract: Classical software effort distribution models, including the PNR family and Parr alter native curve, were designed to describe the time distribution of development effort under an implied staffing pattern. This paper proposes a compact refactoring of Parr model as a capacity-aware forecasting layer for agile projects. The contribution is deliberately narrower than a full causal theory of project dynamics. A normalized Parr shaped latent effort demand is combined with an observed or planned capacity trajectory. The resulting model forecasts aggregate progress, completion time, capacity deficit, and capacity slack without assuming that the same internal activity path is followed under resource restriction. The model uses a small parameter set such as total effort K, a Parr shape parameter, an origin constant c that can match nonzero initial staffing, and the capacity trajectory. A discrete sprint formulation is provided, together with a calibration method from ordinary Scrum records and a rolling origin validation protocol against simple management baselines.

### [278] [A Single Patch Is Not Enough: Deterministic Fusion of Repair Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01597)
*Boyang Yang,Xiangliang Hu,Luyao Ren,Yanjun Chen,Bach Le,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé,Haoye Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PatchFusion提出了一种确定性原子证据融合方法，通过复用候选补丁间的编辑原子证据来选择和构造最终补丁，无需测试或LLM评判。在三个基准上优于现有方法，能以极低成本达到接近候选池上限的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM编码智能体常用pass@k评估，但实际开发中只应用单个补丁。pass@k到pass@1的差距是一个"生成后"问题：候选补丁池可能包含正确补丁，但系统需决定建议哪一个。现有方法（排序、测试过滤、LLM评判）未能确定性复用共享编辑原子证据来同时选择和构造最终补丁。

Method: 提出PatchFusion，一种确定性原子证据融合方法。首先将全差异一致性融合为修复邻域，选择可审计的代表性补丁，然后应用证据约束融合（ECF）保留重复编辑原子并修剪不支持的部分。整个过程不依赖测试结果。

Result: 在PatchFuseBench上，PatchFusion在SWE-bench Verified解决426/500个bug，SWE-bench Multilingual解决236/300个，Defects4J达到87/371个合理补丁。在所有三个基准上优于每个匹配的候选池选择器。恢复41和27个没有单一来源能解决的bug（比最佳单一来源多30和18个）。消融研究表明ECF增加了+5/+6/+9个已解决bug，且无性能退化。

Conclusion: 跨候选证据比基于测试和LLM的选择器能恢复更多正确补丁，成本低数个数量级。在两个SWE-bench基准上分别达到候选池可达上限的96.2%和89.7%。证明确定性原子证据融合是有效且经济的补丁选择方案。

Abstract: Modern LLM coding agents are commonly evaluated using pass@k, but developers typically apply a single final patch in real-world settings. This pass@k-to-pass@1 gap is a post-generation problem: a candidate patch pool may contain a correct patch, but the system must decide which one to suggest to developers. Existing post-generation approaches mainly rank whole candidates, filter them with tests, or query an LLM judge, but none deterministically reuse shared edit-atom evidence to both select and construct the final patch. Thus, we propose PatchFusion, a deterministic atomic evidence fusion approach for candidate patches that consults no test outcome at decision time. PatchFusion first fuses whole-diff agreement into a repair neighborhood, selects an auditable representative, and then applies evidence-constrained fusion (ECF) to retain repeated edit atoms and prune unsupported parts. To evaluate this setting, we build PatchFuseBench, a fixed-pool benchmark covering SWE-bench Verified, SWE-bench Multilingual, and Defects4J candidate patches.
  On PatchFuseBench, PatchFusion solves 426/500 bugs on SWE-bench Verified and 236/300 on SWE-bench Multilingual, and reaches 87/371 plausible patches on Defects4J, outperforming every matched candidate-pool selector on all three. PatchFusion recovers 41 and 27 bugs that no single source solves (30 and 18 more over the best single source). Ablation studies show that ECF adds +5/+6/+9 solved bugs by recovering in-pool repairs that selection misses, with no observed regression, and that PatchFusion's gains remain stable as candidate pools are resampled. On these complementary multi-source pools, cross-candidate evidence recovers more correct patches than the test-based and LLM-based selectors we evaluate, at orders-of-magnitude lower cost, reaching within 96.2% and 89.7% of the candidate-reachable ceiling on the two SWE-bench benchmarks.

### [279] [AgentFlow: Building Agent Dependency Graphs for Static Analysis of Agent Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01640)
*Shenao Wang,Xinyi Hou,Yanjie Zhao,Xiao Cheng,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出AgentFlow，首个针对LLM agent程序的静态分析框架。通过构建Agent Dependency Graph (ADG) 来捕捉agent程序中的新型依赖关系，支持Agent BOM生成和prompt-to-tool风险检测。在5个框架、5,399个真实agent程序上的评估表明，该方法能恢复更丰富的agent实体和依赖，发现238个风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM agent程序依赖框架定义的特殊语义（如工具装饰器、agent交接声明），传统静态分析和依赖追踪工具无法有效恢复这些agent特有的依赖关系，导致agent程序难以被理解、治理和安全审计。

Conclusion: ADG为理解、治理和保障新兴agent软件提供了实用的基础，证明了图驱动方法在agent程序静态分析中的有效性。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly developed as source-code applications built on agent frameworks. These agent programs combine conventional host-language code with framework-defined semantics for models, prompts, tools, memory, and multi-agent orchestration logic. As a result, their behavior depends not only on traditional control and data flows, but also on a new class of agent dependencies. Such dependencies are often expressed as framework-induced semantics, such as agent constructors, tool decorators, and agent handoff declarations, making them difficult to recover with existing static analysis or dependency tracking tools. In this paper, we present AgentFlow, the first static analysis framework for recovering and analyzing agent dependencies from agent programs. AgentFlow constructs an Agent Dependency Graph (ADG), a framework-agnostic graph representation that represents agents, prompts, models, capabilities, memory states, and control policies as typed nodes, and captures their component-dependency, control-flow, and data-flow dependencies as typed edges. Built on ADGs, AgentFlow supports a range of analyses for agent governance and security, including Agent Bill of Materials (BOM) generation and prompt-to-tool risk detection. We implement AgentFlow for five representative agent frameworks and evaluate it on AgentZoo, a corpus of 5,399 real-world agent programs. Our evaluation shows that AgentFlow recovers richer agent entities and dependencies than existing AST-based agent static analysis tools, generates more dependency-aware Agent BOMs, and uncovers 238 taint-style prompt-to-tool risks in real-world agent programs. These results show that ADG provides a practical foundation for understanding, governing, and securing emerging agent software.
